msg:Terrible stay.
I went to Gaoming to play that day, and I didn't plan to stay there. Because the children had fun with their friends, I decided to stay for one night after lunch and leave the next day, and then I booked this hotel immediately.
Since it was the National Day holiday, I didn't compare it carefully, so I looked at the one-night price of more than 800 and booked it immediately. I thought it would not be bad, but I was wrong. We booked a suite in the annex building of the villa, maybe the main building would be better.
This villa sub-building is actually rebuilt with more than a dozen townhouses, one of which is about 4 floors, sharing a staircase in the villa. As soon as you walk in the building, there is a musty smell, it is a country house.
After entering the room, it is big enough, about 90 square meters by visual inspection. There are two toilets in total (one is at the entrance of the gate for unknown purpose), and the other toilet is bigger than the living room. It is estimated that the layout of the original villa has been changed somehow, and part of the space has been changed into a corridor.
The most troublesome thing is that the facilities in the room are outdated. The sofa and the bed look like they have been used for ten or eight years. The white light in the hall and the desk lamp in the room are broken, and the phone in the room is not working, so I can't find the front desk. It can only be called through the platform phone. The two calls were made several times, but no one answered or hung up. Later, I complained through the platform, and the feedback said that it might be too busy to connect during the festival. Call it again, I guess it's hung up. I reported the problem and said that someone would be sent to fix it, but in fact, no one came when I left the next day, and the lights and phones were still broken. There is no feedback. This service is really the worst among the high-star hotels I have ever stayed in. I thought it would be okay to do something with lights at night.
The hall is not big, with two raised sofas, two stools and a table. Old, do not want to sit.
The window of the toilet is broken, there is dust in the corner of the wall, and there is a dead cockroach. Found ants on the bed while sleeping. The color of the drying rack faded, and the next day I found that the washed clothes were all stained.
To sum up, this villa is a product that no one usually lives in, and then it is launched at a high price to deceive people during holidays. This hotel should have been built for a long time. Although it was introduced that it was refurbished in 2019, the main body is still dilapidated and will never live again.
